<Text>This is more of a review for my club fitting, with Nick, than it is for the store, though I love the store, itself, and it's convenient location.

Did you ever just wish you could find that one person; that old (he's not that old) wise, golf sage, whose been around the game, his whole life, and could tell you just what clubs are right for you and your swing?  Someone who could probably make alot of money hawking training aids on an infomercial, but who could never do that in a million years, because he's too sincere and loves the game of golf, too much?  Someone who'd rather just sincerely help people get better?  That's how I see Nick.

I have had a few fittings, though never by anyone I had a lot of confidence in; club pros and a Titleist rep.  None of them seemed overly knowledgeable or terribly interested in my swing.  They just picked the prettiest club, watched a few swings, and said "go with that one."

It was a whole other story with Nick. He spent over an hour with me.  I hit, probably, 50 shots.  He analyzed most of them on the swing tracker and used data to show me how the various clubs were responding to my swing.  He carefully considered what I told him about my game (you've got to be honest about it if you want the right clubs).  I probably hit 10 different combos of shafts and heads.  I ended up with a set that feels fantastic and can't wait to hit them.

Nick has made his own golf clubs.  He works on them, all day, in the shop.  He's a savant about the equipment and speaks to it in nuanced and informed ways.  If you truly want a good fitting, go see Nick.< /Text>< Gmap_id>

Taco Grill is located in the same spot as the old Cabo Grill. At the time of this review, the signage wasn't replaced. I had 3 asada tacos and it was nice that it wasn't heavily salted. The tacos were larger in size than the smaller ones that you find at other Taquerias. I have to admit I was once a fan of this chewy asada meat but having been spoiled with the newer generation of trendy tacos that uses high quality juicy cuts, the chew factor gets in my way of enjoyment. The staff is friendly and the food comes out quick. The small parking lot can feel cramped when manuevering so be careful when backing out.< /Text>

<Text>Buyer beware! The longer you rent from Jefferson Self Storage the more you will pay! They advertise low prices to get you in the door, next thing you know your rates are being increased above the average yearly rate of inflation. I have been a loyal customer for two years now, never missed a payment and now I'm being charged $168 a month for a 10x10 drive up unit, non climate controlled, while a new customer can get the exact same unit right now for $145 a month. How is that fair? Beware of their cheaper prices, their units are mediocre, the light in my unit has been out for two years now and they have a major pest issue being right next to a vacant lot in the back.
**Update 4/5/2021 Found a rotting, dead rat in the corner of my storage unit upon clearing it out. Rat poop all love the place and rat poison trash left in my unit by Jefferson Self storage, see pictures below. This is absolutely un-satisfactory for paying $167 a month for a 10x10 drive up unit. On top of barely any security cameras, limited hours of use, and a major rodent infestation problem it's obvious this storage company is absorbing all of the profits from increasing rent every year and not updating their services and storage. So you and I, the consumer pay more but get the same below standard service in return.

< text>
TL;DR
I would never recommend coming here, the frozen food from a place like Trader Joe's will be 10x better, and much cheaper, than the food served here (And the food served here will still not be any better than frozen food from a place like Vons).

Long version
============

I'm very unsure why this is 4.2 stars rn. I ordered a chicken parmesan and it wasn't chicken cutlet, it was grilled chicken - but okay, maybe that's their take on that dish so I'll let that confusing choice slide. However, the bread was terrible. It was not good Italian bread, it was mushy and soggy bun-like bread. The chicken was tough, and the sauce had minimal flavor. I ordered a lasagna and, rather than a meat sauce, it just came with the same flavorless red sauce and two meatballs (Meatballs??). The meatballs were very mediocre in taste, and had a consistency of a paste/playdoh (The awful consistency ruined any taste consideration, but it was about as flavorless as the sauce by percentile. I.e., 0th percentile). It could not have been made from fresh ground beef, the worst cook couldn't make it that consistency using ground beef. It must've been the cheapest possible frozen meatball available (There are definitely better frozen meatballs out there). The pasta was very bad - rubbery even, though the cheese was fine. I don't know how it would be possible to mess up cheese though, so it doesn't qualify as "impossibly bad", perhaps just "as bad as possible".</text>

<date>1608770144797<//date><Rating>1</Rating>< Review>
I have always enjoyed going to this Barnes and Noble -- but today was an exception and I will not be going back.  I have not been shopping much but got masked up for the big shopping day. I was happily shopping ( a nice employee Kyle actually helped me find the first thing on my list very quickly, and he was very friendly and nice) when I got a text to look for a Gingerbread Kit...thinking they would be in the gift or Christmas area I scurried off to look.  All of a sudden I heard shouting that I could not understand through the employee's mask - I looked to see who she was talking to and saw no one - so I continued on my way to shop the gift section.  Another male employee comes up shouting that I can't cut through the line...I look around seeing no people or any line where I am looking -  only gifts but they are both shouting at me which was quite embarrassing.  I ask about the Gingerbread Kit and they do not have any this year.  First of all I saw no line where I was physically walking and I was not even within 25 feet of a cash register...second of all -- why are they shouting at people shopping the gift section at Christmas?  Would it be odd to be looking for a gift?  What gave them the impression I was in line or checking out?  I would have liked to have bought nothing, but promised I would get some books for my son's girlfriend and had no other option in shopping. So I looked for one more gift (obviously not in the gift section as that seemed to be the whole fuss  the employees not wanting customers to look at the gifts...paid and left. My cashier was very sweet but honestly it only takes one apple to sour the bunch and here we had two bad apples.  I will shop Amazon in the future or look for a brick and mortar store that wants business. I found this visit, embarrassing and the employees rude...perhaps they could have asked if they could help me find something...or politely asked if I knew I was in a line (with no people).   I just do not get it - seems these masks are taking away people sense of kindness as they hide behind them.</Review>

This is one of our family's favourite places to frequent. They have comfy chairs (that you often have to be quick to get one) and a cafe inside. < Text>
STARBUCKS: This review is strictly on my experience with STARBUCKS located in this B&N location. The person taking orders did not look pleased with being there. I would not have noticed this but I'm also in the service industry mostly hotels. She took my name like all other starbucks but it was not used to call my order, at all. My name was not used for my drink. I had to wait for my sandwich to be prepared which was over cooked when I got it making the bread rubbery and hard to eat. The part of my visit that prompted me to write this review was that my order sat on the counter for ? amount of time, when I asked about it I was told the order was placed on the order counter and my name was called. I was at the pick up counter where we all know to go for our orders??? My sandwich was at the pick-up counter when I went up to ask about it. Who trains this staff? Maybe the staff that day is not ready to work with the public. The response I got from both employees when I asked about my order was snide and unprofessional. I never thought I'd see someone at this capacity act with such entitlement.

P.S. This B&N is beautiful inside and out. Its located near everything. I found a book here that I needed for a Business course I was taking. I will use this location for any hard copy publications in the future, but I'll probably pass on Starbucks here, Jamba Juice is just across from there in the food court, yum!   GO Gators!!!<//Text>
